Source Code

These source code files are an attempted reconstruction of Sundance revision 306, the Apollo 9 LM (Lunar Module) AGC (Apollo Guidance Computer) flight software, created from binary dumps of original core rope program modules, as follows:
  • B1 — Revision 292
  • B2 — Revision 302
  • B3 — Revision 302
  • B4 — Revision 302
  • B5 — Revision 292
  • B6 — Revision 306
These dumps were then modified using memos, checklists, observed address changes, and the Sundance GSOPs to get the entire program to match Sundance revision 306 as closely as possible. Without more information, it is not possible to say how close it actually is; however, this code should be quite close. It is capable of flying the whole Apollo 9 mission using the original checklists and padload. Since only binary dumps (rather than listings) of Sundance are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

014549,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
014550,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
014551,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of an attempt to reconstruct Sundance revision 306
014552,000005:                                                                                                  ##              as closely as possible with available information. Sundance
014553,000006:                                                                                                  ##              306 is the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
014554,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 9. This program was created
014555,000008:                                                                                                  ##              using the mixed-revision SundanceXXX as a starting point, and
014556,000009:                                                                                                  ##              pulling back features from Luminary 69 believed to have been
014557,000010:                                                                                                  ##              added based on memos, checklists, observed address changes,
014558,000011:                                                                                                  ##              or the Sundance GSOPs.
014559,000012:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
014560,000013:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
014561,000014:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
014562,000015:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-07-24 MAS  Created from SundanceXXX.

014565,000018: 
014566,000019:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
014567,000020:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
014568,000021:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
014569,000022:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
014570,000023: 
014571,000024:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
014572,000025: 
014573,000026:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
014574,000027:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
014575,000028:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
014576,000029:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
014577,000030:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
014578,000031:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
014579,000032:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
014580,000033:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
014581,000034:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
014582,000035: 
014583,000036:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
014584,000037:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
014585,000038:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
014586,000039:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
014587,000040:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
014588,000041:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
014589,000042:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

014624,000077: 
014625,000078:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
014626,000079: 
014627,000080:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
014628,000081:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
014629,000082:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
014630,000083:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
014631,000084:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
014632,000085: 
014633,000086:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
014634,000087:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
014635,000088:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
014636,000089:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
014637,000090: 
014638,000091:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
014639,000092:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
014640,000093:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
014641,000094:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
014642,000095:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
014643,000096: 
014644,000097:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
014645,000098:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
014646,000099:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
014647,000100:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
014648,000101:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
014649,000102:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
014650,000103:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
014651,000104:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
014652,000105:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
014653,000106:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
014654,000107:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
014655,000108:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
014656,000109:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
014657,000110:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
014658,000111: 
014659,000112:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
014660,000113:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
014661,000114:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
014662,000115: 
014663,000116: 
014664,000117:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
014665,000118: 
014666,000119:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
014667,000120:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
014668,000121:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
014669,000122: 
014670,000123:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
014671,000124:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
014672,000125:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
014673,000126:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
014674,000127:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
014675,000128:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
014676,000129:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
014677,000130: 
014678,000131:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
014679,000132:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
014680,000133: 
014681,000134: 
014682,000135:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
014683,000136: 
014684,000137:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
014685,000138:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
014686,000139:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
014687,000140:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
014688,000141: 
014689,000142: 
014690,000143:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
014691,000144: 
014692,000145:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
014693,000146:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
014694,000147:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
014695,000148:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
014696,000149: 
014697,000150:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
014698,000151:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
014699,000152: 
014700,000153: 
014701,000154:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
014702,000155: 
014703,000156:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
014704,000157:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
014705,000158: 
014706,000159:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
014707,000160:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
014708,000161:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
014709,000162:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
014710,000163: 
014711,000164:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
014712,000165:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
014713,000166: 
014714,000167:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
014715,000168:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
014716,000169:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
014717,000170:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
014718,000171: 
014719,000172:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
014720,000173:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
014721,000174: 
014722,000175:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
014723,000176:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
014724,000177: 
014725,000178:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
014726,000179: 
014727,000180:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
014728,000181:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
014729,000182:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
014730,000183:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
014731,000184: 
014732,000185:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
014733,000186:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
014734,000187: 
014735,000188:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
014736,000189:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
014737,000190: 
014738,000191: 
014739,000192:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
014740,000193:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
014741,000194:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
014742,000195:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

014752,000205:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Actually, this quotation is from Henry VI, Part 2, Act IV, Scene VII. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

014760,000213:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
014761,000214: 
014762,000215: 
014763,000216:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
014764,000217: 
014765,000218:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
014766,000219:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
014767,000220:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
014768,000221:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
014769,000222:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
014770,000223:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
014771,000224:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
014772,000225:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
014773,000226:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
014774,000227:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
014775,000228:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
014776,000229:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
014777,000230:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
014778,000231:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
014779,000232:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
014780,000233:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
014781,000234:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
014782,000235:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
014783,000236:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
014784,000237:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
014785,000238:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
014786,000239:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
014787,000240:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE+1
014788,000241:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
014789,000242:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
014790,000243:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
014791,000244:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
014792,000245:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
014793,000246:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
014794,000247:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
014795,000248:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
014796,000249:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
014797,000250:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
014798,000251:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
014799,000252:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
014800,000253:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
014801,000254:

014827,000280:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN  =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
014828,000281:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMIN-1.

014830,000283:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2  =      VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)

014832,000285:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMIN+1.

014862,000315:                                                                                                  #  SEPMNRET =      TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN
014863,000316: 
014864,000317:                                                                                                  #  TEM5     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
014865,000318:                                                                                                  #  NOUNADD  =      TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
014866,000319: 
014867,000320:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM  ERASE                  TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
014868,000321:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
014869,000322:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
014870,000323:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
014871,000324:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
014872,000325:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
014873,000326:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
014874,000327:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
014875,000328:                                                                                                  #  RUTMXTEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN ONLY)
014876,000329:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
014877,000330: 
014878,000331: 
014879,000332:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
014880,000333: 
014881,000334:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
014882,000335:                                                                                                  #  BUF, +1, +2
014883,000336:                                                                                                  #  BUF2, +1, +2
014884,000337:                                                                                                  #  MPTEMP
014885,000338:                                                                                                  #  ADDRWD
014886,000339:                                                                                                  #    END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
014887,000340: 
014888,000341: 
014889,000342:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
014890,000343: 
014891,000344:                                                                                                  #  DSPCNT   ERASE                  COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
014892,000345:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK   ERASE                  BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
014893,000346:                                                                                                  #                                                                          RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
014894,000347:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
014895,000348: 
014896,000349: 
014897,000350:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
014898,000351:

014900,000353:                                                                                                  #  DSRUPTEM =      WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
014901,000354:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP2 =      RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
014902,000355:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
014903,000356: 
014904,000357:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
014905,000358:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
014906,000359:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
014907,000360:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
014908,000361:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
014909,000362:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
014910,000363:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
014911,000364:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
014912,000365:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
014913,000366:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
014914,000367:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
014915,000368:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

014917,000370: 
014918,000371: 
014919,000372:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
014920,000373:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
014921,000374:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
014922,000375:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
014923,000376:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
014924,000377:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
014925,000378: 
014926,000379:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
014927,000380:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
014928,000381:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
014929,000382:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
014930,000383:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
014931,000384:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
014932,000385: 
014933,000386:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
014934,000387:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
014935,000388:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
014936,000389:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
014937,000390:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
014938,000391:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
014939,000392:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
014940,000393:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
014941,000394:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
014942,000395:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
014943,000396:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
014944,000397:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
014945,000398: 
014946,000399: 
014947,000400:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
014948,000401: 
014949,000402:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
014950,000403:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
014951,000404:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
014952,000405:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
014953,000406:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
014954,000407:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)
014955,000408:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
014956,000409:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
014957,000410:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
014958,000411:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
014959,000412:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
014960,000413:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
014961,000414:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
014962,000415:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
014963,000416: 
014964,000417: 
014965,000418:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
014966,000419:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
014967,000420:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
014968,000421:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
014969,000422:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
014970,000423:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
014971,000424:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
014972,000425:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
014973,000426:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
014974,000427:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
014975,000428:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
014976,000429:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
014977,000430: 
014978,000431: 
014979,000432:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
014980,000433: 
014981,000434:                                                                                                  #             KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
014982,000435:                                                                                                  #             VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
014983,000436:                                                                                                  #             OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
014984,000437:

015671,001124: 
015672,001125: 41,2350           04157        GOALMCYC           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #  NEEDED BECAUSE BANKJUMP CANT HANDLE F/F.
015673,001126: 
015674,001127: 
015675,001128: 41,2351           04674        GODSPALM           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015676,001129: 41,2352           61533                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
015677,001130: 
015678,001131:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
015679,001132:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
015680,001133:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
015681,001134:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
015682,001135:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
015683,001136:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
015684,001137: 
015685,001138:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
015686,001139:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
015687,001140: 
015688,001141:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
015689,001142: 
015690,001143:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
015691,001144:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
015692,001145:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
015693,001146: 
015694,001147:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
015695,001148:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
015696,001149:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
015697,001150:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
015698,001151:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
015699,001152:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
015700,001153: 
015701,001154:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
015702,001155:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
015703,001156:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
015704,001157:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
015705,001158:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
015706,001159: 
015707,001160:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
015708,001161:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
015709,001162:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
015710,001163:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
015711,001164:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
015712,001165:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
015713,001166:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
015714,001167:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
015715,001168: 
015716,001169: 
015717,001170:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
015718,001171:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
015719,001172:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
015720,001173: 
015721,001174: 
015722,001175:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
015723,001176:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
015724,001177: 
015725,001178:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
015726,001179:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
015727,001180: 
015728,001181:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
015729,001182: 41,2353           45025        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
015730,001183: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
015731,001184: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
015732,001185: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2                                     
015733,001186: 41,2357           56132                           XCH      BUF        +2                         
015734,001187: 41,2360           45026        DSPAB              CS       ONE                                   
015735,001188: 41,2361           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
015736,001189: 41,2362           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
015737,001190: 41,2363           40001                           CS       1                                     
015738,001191: 41,2364           56131                           XCH      BUF        +1                         
015739,001192: 41,2365           02443        DSPA               TC       DECTEST                               
015740,001193: 41,2366           02466                           TC       TSTFORDP                              
015741,001194: 41,2367           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
015742,001195: 41,2370           40000                           CS       0                                     
015743,001196: 41,2371           56130        DSPCOM1            XCH      BUF

016036,001489:                                                                                                  #  AS TWO POSITIVE DECIMAL INTEGERS IN RXD1-RXD2 AND RXD4-RXD5 (RXD3 IS
016037,001490:                                                                                                  #  BLANKED). THE INTEGER IN THE LOWER NUMBERED ADDRESS IS DISPLAYED IN

016246,001699:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOSE VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
016247,001700:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
016248,001701:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS. IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
016249,001702:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO .  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
016250,001703:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
016251,001704:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

016839,002292: 
016840,002293: 42,3560           44113        FORCEV25           CS       OCT31                                 #  FORCE VERB 25 TO BE EXECUTED BY RECYCLE
016841,002294: 42,3561           55042                           TS       VERBSAVE                              #   IN CASE OPERATOR EXECUTED A LOWER LOAD
016842,002295: 42,3562           04157                           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #   VERB.  ALARM AND RECYCLE.
016843,002296: 42,3563                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
016844,002297: 
016845,002298:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
016846,002299:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
016847,002300:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
016848,002301:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
016849,002302:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
016850,002303: 
016851,002304:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
016852,002305:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
016853,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
016854,002307:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
016855,002308:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
016856,002309:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
016857,002310:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
016858,002311: 
016859,002312:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
016860,002313:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
016861,002314:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
016862,002315: 
016863,002316:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
016864,002317:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
016865,002318: 
016866,002319:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
016867,002320:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
016868,002321: 
016869,002322:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW
016870,002323: 41,3223                                           SETLOC   ENDRUTIN

016995,002448:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
016996,002449:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
016997,002450:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
016998,002451: 
016999,002452:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
017000,002453: 
017001,002454:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
017002,002455:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
017003,002456:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
017004,002457: 
017005,002458:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
017006,002459:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
017007,002460:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
017008,002461: 
017009,002462: 41,3346           34331        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
017010,002463: 41,3347           55000                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
017011,002464: 41,3350           31050                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
017012,002465: 41,3351           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
017013,002466: 41,3352           31020                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
017014,002467: 41,3353           04714                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
017015,002468: 41,3354           03356                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
017016,002469: 41,3355           05225        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

017192,002645:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB ENTRY INTO DSREL.

017378,002831:                                                                                                  #  VBRQWAIT ENTERS REQUEST TO WAITLIST FOR ANY ADDRESS WITH ANY DELAY.

017391,002844:                                                                                                  #  TC ENDOFJOB INTO MPAC+3. IT WILL TAKE TIME DELAY OUT OF MPAC+4 AND
017392,002845:                                                                                                  #  LEAVE IT IN A, INHINT AND TC MPAC.

017408,002861:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CONTROL, WITH CHRPRIO.
