017416,002869: 
017417,002870:                                                                                                  #  VBRESEQ WAKES ENDIDLE AT SAME LINE AS FINAL ENTER OF LOAD (L+3).
017418,002871:                                                                                                  #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
017419,002872:                                                                                                  #   DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE. SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS,PLEASE PERFORM,
017420,002873:                                                                                                  #   OR PLEASE MARK VERBS BECAUSE THEY ALREADY USE L+3 IN ANOTHER CONTEXT.)
017421,002874: 
017422,002875: 40,3561           45030        VBRESEQ            CS       ZERO                                  #  MAKE IT LOOK LIKE DATA IN.
017423,002876: 40,3562           03545                           TC       VBPROC     +1                         
017424,002877: 
017425,002878: 
017426,002879:                                                                                                  #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE,
017427,002880:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
017428,002881: 
017429,002882:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
017430,002883: 
017431,002884:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
017432,002885: 
017433,002886:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
017434,002887:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
017435,002888:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
017436,002889:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
017437,002890: 
017438,002891:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
017439,002892:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
017440,002893:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
017441,002894: 
017442,002895:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
017443,002896:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
017444,002897:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
017445,002898:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
017446,002899:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
017447,002900:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
017448,002901:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
017449,002902:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
017450,002903:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
017451,002904:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
017452,002905:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
017453,002906: 
017454,002907: 40,3563           45024        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
017455,002908: 40,3564           00006                           EXTEND                                         
017456,002909: 40,3565           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
017457,002910: 40,3566           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
017458,002911: 40,3567           35011                           CAF      BIT14                                 
017459,002912: 40,3570           71022                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
017460,002913: 40,3571           10000                           CCS      A                                     
017461,002914: 40,3572           03601                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
017462,002915: 40,3573           04471        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
017463,002916: 40,3574           11043                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
017464,002917: 40,3575           03577                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
017465,002918: 40,3576           05225                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
017466,002919: 40,3577           04674                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
017467,002920: 40,3600           20746                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
017468,002921: 40,3601           35030        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
017469,002922: 40,3602           55013                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
017470,002923: 40,3603           11043                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
017471,002924: 40,3604           05225                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
017472,002925: 40,3605           04514                           TC       RELDSP1                               
017473,002926: 40,3606           05225                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
017474,002927: 
017475,002928: 40,3607                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
017476,002929: 
017477,002930: 
017478,002931:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
017479,002932:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
017480,002933:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
017481,002934:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
017482,002935:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
017483,002936: 
017484,002937:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
017485,002938:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
017486,002939:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
017487,002940: 
017488,002941:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
017489,002942:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
017490,002943: 
017491,002944:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
017492,002945:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
017493,002946:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
017494,002947:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
017495,002948:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
017496,002949: 
017497,002950:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
017498,002951:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
017499,002952:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
017500,002953:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
017501,002954: 
017502,002955:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
017503,002956:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
017504,002957:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
017505,002958:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
017506,002959:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
017507,002960:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
017508,002961:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
017509,002962: 
017510,002963:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
017511,002964:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
017512,002965: 
017513,002966:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
017514,002967:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
017515,002968: 
017516,002969:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
017517,002970:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
017518,002971: 
017519,002972:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
017520,002973:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
017521,002974:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
017522,002975:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
017523,002976:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
017524,002977:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
017525,002978:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
017526,002979: 
017527,002980:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL
017528,002981:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
017529,002982:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
017530,002983:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
017531,002984:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
017532,002985:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
017533,002986:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
017534,002987:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
017535,002988:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
017536,002989:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
017537,002990: 
017538,002991:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
017539,002992:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
017540,002993: 
017541,002994:    4166                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
017542,002995: 
017543,002996:    4166                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
017544,002997:    4166           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017545,002998:    4167           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
017546,002999:    4170           35011                           CAF      BIT14                                 
017547,003000:    4171           71022                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
017548,003001:    4172           61013                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
017549,003002:    4173           10000                           CCS      A                                     
017550,003003:    4174           00002                           TC       Q                                     #  DSP SYST BLOCKED. RET TO 1+ CALLING LOC
017551,003004:    4175           35026                           CAF      ONE                                   #  DSP SYST AVAILABLE
017552,003005:    4176           60002        NVSBCOM            AD       Q                                     
017553,003006:    4177           55040                           TS       NVQTEM                                #  2+ CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM
017554,003007:    4200           23023                           LXCH     MONSAVE2                              #  STORE NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017555,003008:    4201           04216                           TC       KILMONON                              #  TURN ON KILL MONITOR BIT
017556,003009:    4202           34213        NVSUBCOM           CAF      NVSBBBNK

017566,003019:    4213     1000                                  EBANK=   DSPCOUNT

017569,003022:    4214     4213               PINSUPBT           =        NVSBBBNK                              #  CONTAINS THE PINBALL SUPERBITS.
017570,003023: 
017571,003024:    4214           53041        NVSUBEND           DXCH     NVQTEM                                #  NVBNKTEM MUST = NVQTEM+1
017572,003025:    4215           05235                           TC       SUPDXCHZ                              #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING
017573,003026: 
017574,003027: 
017575,003028: 41,3511                                           SETLOC   ENDRQWT    +1                         
017576,003029: 
017577,003030: 41,3511                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
017578,003031:                                                                                                  #  BLANKDSP BLANKS DISPLAY ACCORDING TO OPTION NUMBER IN NVTEMP AS FOLLOWS
017579,003032:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
017580,003033: 
017581,003034: 41,3511           65032        BLANKDSP           AD       SEVEN                                 #  7,8,9,OR 10 (A HAD 0,1,2,OR 3)
017582,003035: 41,3512           00004                           INHINT

017597,003050: 41,3531           55003                           TS       NOUNREG                               #             -2

017600,003053: 41,3534           55000                           TS       DSPCOUNT

017602,003055: 41,3536           03561                           TC       ENTSET     -2                         #  ZEROS REQRET
017603,003056: 
017604,003057: 41,3537           33563        NVSUB1             CAF      ENTSET                                #  IN BANK

017606,003059: 41,3541           10123                           CCS      NVTEMP                                #  WHAT NOW
017607,003060: 41,3542           03546                           TC       +4                                    #  NORMAL NVSUB CALL (EXECUTE VN OR PASTE)
017608,003061: 41,3543           02351                           TC       GODSPALM                              
017609,003062: 41,3544           03511                           TC       BLANKDSP                              #  BLANK DISPLAY AS SPECIFIED
017610,003063: 41,3545           02351                           TC       GODSPALM

017612,003065: 41,3547           70123                           MASK     NVTEMP                                
017613,003066: 41,3550           54157                           TS       MPAC       +3                         #  TEMP FOR NOUN (CANT USE MPAC. DSPDECVN
017614,003067: 41,3551           30123                           CA       NVTEMP                                #                  USES MPAC, +1, +2
017615,003068: 41,3552           54023                           TS       EDOP                                  #  RIGHT 7
017616,003069: 41,3553           30023                           CA       EDOP                                  
017617,003070: 41,3554           54160                           TS       MPAC       +4                         #  TEMP FOR VERB (CANT USE MPAC+1. DSPDECVN
017618,003071:                                                                                                  #                 USES MPAC, +1, +2).
017619,003072: 41,3555           10157                           CCS      MPAC       +3                         #  TEST NOUN
017620,003073: 41,3556           03564                           TC       NVSUB2                                #  IF NOUN NOT +0, GO ON
017621,003074: 41,3557           30160                           CA       MPAC       +4                         
017622,003075: 41,3560           02337                           TC       UPDATVB    -1                         #  IF NOUN = +0, DISPLAY VERB . THEN RETURN
017623,003076: 41,3561           35030                           CAF      ZERO                                  #  ZERO REQRET SO THAT PASTED VERBS CAN
017624,003077: 41,3562           55014                           TS       REQRET                                #  BE EXECUTED BY OPERATOR.
017625,003078: 41,3563           04214        ENTSET             TC       NVSUBEND                              
017626,003079: 41,3564           10160        NVSUB2             CCS      MPAC       +4                         #  TEST VERB
017627,003080: 41,3565           03571                           TC       +4                                    #  IF VERB NOT +0, GO ON
017628,003081: 41,3566           30157                           CA       MPAC       +3                         
017629,003082: 41,3567           02317                           TC       UPDATNN    -1                         #  IF VERB = +0, DISPLAY NOUN. THEN RETURN
017630,003083: 41,3570           04214                           TC       NVSUBEND                              
017631,003084: 41,3571           30156                           CA       MPAC       +2                         #  TEMP FOR MACH CADR TO BE SPEC. (DSPDECVN
017632,003085: 41,3572           54161                           TS       MPAC       +5                         #               USES MPAC, +1, +2)
017633,003086: 41,3573           30160                           CA       MPAC       +4

017635,003088: 41,3575           30157                           CA       MPAC       +3                         #  BOTH AND GO TO ENTPAS0.
017636,003089: 41,3576           02317                           TC       UPDATNN    -1                         
017637,003090: 41,3577           35030                           CAF      ZERO                                  
017638,003091: 41,3600           55015                           TS       LOADSTAT                              #  SET FOR WAITING FOR DATA CONDITION
017639,003092: 41,3601           55016                           TS       CLPASS

017641,003094: 41,3603           30161                           CA       MPAC       +5                         #  RESTORES MACH CADR TO BE SPEC TO MPAC+2
017642,003095: 41,3604           54156                           TS       MPAC       +2                         #  FOR USE IN INTMCTBS (IN ENTPAS0).
017643,003096: 41,3605           02035        ENDNVSB1           TC       ENTPAS0                               
017644,003097: 
017645,003098: 
017646,003099:                                                                                                  #  IF INTERNAL MACH CADR TO BE SPECIFIED, MPAC+2 WILL BE PLACED INTO
017647,003100:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS ).
017648,003101: 
017649,003102: 
017650,003103:    4216                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
017651,003104:    4216                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
017652,003105:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
017653,003106:    4216           35010        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
017654,003107:    4217           55022                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
017655,003108:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
017656,003109:    4220           00002                           TC       Q                                     
017657,003110: 
017658,003111: 
017659,003112:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
017660,003113:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
017661,003114:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
017662,003115:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
017663,003116:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
017664,003117: 
017665,003118: 
017666,003119:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
017667,003120:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
017668,003121:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
017669,003122:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
017670,003123:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
017671,003124:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
017672,003125:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
017673,003126:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
017674,003127:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
017675,003128:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
017676,003129: 
017677,003130: 
017678,003131:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
017679,003132:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
017680,003133:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
017681,003134:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
017682,003135:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
017683,003136:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
017684,003137: 
017685,003138:    4221           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
017686,003139:    4222           04232                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
017687,003140:    4223           04236                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
017688,003141:    4224           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
017689,003142:    4225           75062                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
017690,003143:    4226           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
017691,003144:    4227           55043                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
017692,003145:    4230           05203                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
017693,003146: 
017694,003147: 
017695,003148:    4231           05225        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
017696,003149: 
017697,003150: 
017698,003151:    4232           11043        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
017699,003152:    4233           04241                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
017700,003153:    4234           00002                           TC       Q                                     
017701,003154:    4235           04241                           TC       DSPABORT                              
017702,003155: 
017703,003156:    4236           11044        ISLIST+0           CCS      DSPLIST                               #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
017704,003157:    4237           04241                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF DSPLIST = +0.
017705,003158:    4240           00002                           TC       Q                                     
017706,003159:    4241           05716        DSPABORT           TC       ABORT                                 
017707,003160:    4242           01206                           OCT      01206                                 
017708,003161: 
017709,003162:

017711,003164:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES ENDOFJOB.

017740,003193: 
017741,003194: 
017742,003195:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
017743,003196:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
017744,003197:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.
017745,003198:                                                                                                  #  ANY COMBINATION OF THESE BITS IS ACCEPTED.
017746,003199: 
017747,003200:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT IS RESTORED TO STATE IT WAS IN BEFORE BLANKSUB WAS EXECUTED.
017748,003201:

017751,003204:    4271           35011                           CAF      BIT14

017753,003206:    4273           61013                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
017754,003207:    4274           10000                           CCS      A

017796,003249: 40,3630           05236                           TC       SUPDXCHZ   +1                         #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING

017802,003255: 40,3635           00002                           TC       2

017805,003258: 
017806,003259: 
017807,003260:                                                                                                  #  DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY MODREG DIRECTLY. IT PUTS IN EXEC REQUEST WITH
017808,003261:                                                                                                  #  PRIO 30000 FOR DSPMMJB AND RETURNS TO CALLER.
017809,003262: 
017810,003263:                                                                                                  #  IF MODREG CONTAINS -0, DSPMMJB BLANKS THE MODE LIGHTS.
017811,003264: 
017812,003265:                                                                                                  #  DSPMM MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT CAN BE CALLED VIA BANKCALL.

017816,003269: 04,2000                                           BANK

017850,003303:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED), TERMINATE VERB IS EXECUTED, OR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA VERB IS
017851,003304:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IT WAKES UP JOB THAT DID TC ENDIDLE.

017854,003307:                                                                                                  #  LIGHT IF DSPLIST IS EMPTY (LEAVES KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF NOT EMPTY).

018003,003456: 
018004,003457: 
018005,003458:                                                                                                  #  IF MPAC, +1 ARE EACH +NZ OR +0 AND C(A)=-0, SHORTMP WRONGLY GIVES +0.
018006,003459:                                                                                                  #  IF MPAC, +1 ARE EACH -NZ OR -0 AND C(A)=+0, SHORTMP WRONGLY GIVES +0.
018007,003460:                                                                                                  #  PRSHRTMP FIXES FIRST CASE ONLY, BY MERELY TESTING C(A) AND IF IT = -0,
018008,003461:                                                                                                  #  SETTING RESULT TO -0.
018009,003462:                                                                                                  #   (DO NOT USE PRSHRTMP UNLESS MPAC, +1 ARE EACH +NZ OR +0, AS THEY ARE
018010,003463:                                                                                                  #   WHEN THEY CONTAIN TH E SF CONSTANTS.)
018011,003464:

018013,003466:    4430           10000                           CCS      A                                     
018014,003467:    4431           30135                           CA       MPTEMP                                #  C(A) +, DO REGULAR SHORTMP
018015,003468:    4432           17262                           TCF      SHORTMP    +1                         #  C(A) +0, DO REGULAR SHORTMP
018016,003469:    4433           14431                           TCF      -2                                    #  C(A) -, DO REGULAR SHORTMP
018017,003470:    4434           45030                           CS       ZERO                                  #  C(A) -0, FORCE RESULT TO -0 AND RETURN.
018018,003471:    4435           54154                           TS       MPAC

018031,003484:    4446           00006                           EXTEND                                         
018032,003485:    4447           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
018033,003486:    4450           00002                           TC       Q                                     
018034,003487: 
018035,003488:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
018036,003489: 
018037,003490:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
018038,003491:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
018039,003492:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
018040,003493:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
018041,003494: 
018042,003495:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
018043,003496:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
018044,003497:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
018045,003498:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
018046,003499:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
018047,003500:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
018048,003501:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
018049,003502: 
018050,003503: 
018051,003504:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
018052,003505:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
018053,003506:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
018054,003507:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
018055,003508:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
018056,003509: 
018057,003510: 
018058,003511:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
018059,003512:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
018060,003513:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
018061,003514:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
018062,003515:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
018063,003516: 
018064,003517: 
018065,003518:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
018066,003519:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
018067,003520:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
018068,003521: 
018069,003522: 
018070,003523:                                                                                                  #  .
018071,003524: 
018072,003525: 
018073,003526:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
018074,003527:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
018075,003528:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
018076,003529:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
018077,003530: 
018078,003531: 
018079,003532:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
018080,003533:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
018081,003534:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
018082,003535:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
018083,003536:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
018084,003537:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING
018085,003538:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
018086,003539: 
018087,003540:    4451           44456        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
018088,003541:    4452           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
018089,003542:    4453           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
018090,003543:    4454           04674        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
018091,003544:    4455           10521                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
018092,003545:    4456           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
018093,003546: 
018094,003547:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
018095,003548:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
018096,003549: 
018097,003550: 04,2521                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
018098,003551: 04,2521                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
018099,003552: 04,2521           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
018100,003553: 04,2522           04232                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
018101,003554: 04,2523           04236                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
018102,003555: 04,2524           04406                           TC       RELDSPON                              
018103,003556: 04,2525           30001                           CA       L                                     
018104,003557: 04,2526           55044                           TS       DSPLIST                               
018105,003558: 04,2527           05203        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
018106,003559: 
018107,003560: 
018108,003561:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
018109,003562:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
018110,003563:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
018111,003564:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
018112,003565:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
018113,003566: 
018114,003567:    4457                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
018115,003568:    4457                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
018116,003569:    4457           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
018117,003570:    4460           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
018118,003571:    4461           35011                           CAF      BIT14                                 
018119,003572:    4462           71022                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
018120,003573:    4463           61013                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
018121,003574:    4464           10000                           CCS      A                                     
018122,003575:    4465           14467                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
018123,003576:    4466           14176                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
018124,003577:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
018125,003578:    4467           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
018126,003579:    4470           14451                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
018127,003580: 
018128,003581: 
018129,003582:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
018130,003583:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
018131,003584:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
018132,003585:    4471           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
018133,003586:    4472           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
018134,003587:    4473           45011                           CS       BIT14                                 
018135,003588:    4474           00004                           INHINT                                         
018136,003589:    4475           71022                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
018137,003590:    4476           55022                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
018138,003591:    4477           11044                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
018139,003592:    4500           04502                           TC       +2                                    
018140,003593:    4501           04505                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
018141,003594:    4502           35030                           CAF      ZERO                                  
018142,003595:    4503           57044                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
018143,003596:    4504           05207                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
018144,003597:    4505           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
018145,003598:    4506           45022                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
018146,003599:    4507           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
018147,003600:    4510           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              
018148,003601:    4511           35030                           CAF      ZERO                                  
018149,003602:    4512           55013                           TS       DSPLOCK                               
018150,003603:    4513           00144                           TC       RELRET                                
018151,003604:    4514           56002        RELDSP1            XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0. NO DSPLIST SEARCH.
018152,003605:    4515           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  TURN KEY RLSE LIGHT OFF IF DSPLIST IS
018153,003606:                                                                                                  #  EMPTY. LEAVE KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF

018274,003727: 
018275,003728:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
018276,003729:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
018277,003730:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
018278,003731:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
018279,003732:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
018280,003733:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
018281,003734:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
018282,003735: 
018283,003736: 40,3705                                           SETLOC   DOPROC     +2                         
018284,003737: 40,3705                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

018286,003739: 40,3706           55013                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #  LIGHT RESET LEAVES DSPLOCK UNCHANGED.
018287,003740: 40,3707           00004                           INHINT

018289,003742: 40,3711           00006                           EXTEND                                         
018290,003743: 40,3712           05011                           WOR      DSALMOUT                              #  BIT10 CHAN 11
018291,003744: 40,3713           33774                           CAF      GL+NOATT                              #  LEAVE GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT INTACT,
018292,003745: 40,3714           71037                           MASK     DSPTAB     +11D                       #  TURNING OFF AUTO, HOLD, FREE,
018293,003746: 40,3715           65010                           AD       BIT15                                 #  PROG ALARM, AND TRACKER.
018294,003747: 40,3716           55037                           TS       DSPTAB     +11D                       
018295,003748: 40,3717           45076                           CS       PRIO16                                #  RESET FAIL BITS WHICH GENERATE PROG

018297,003750: 40,3721           65076                           AD       PRIO16                                #  EXISTS, THE ALARM WILL COME BACK.
